### 🛠️ **Tool result**  ·  19:18:59; tool 10ms

```
1	(** * A minimal, executable RV64I model in Coq -- mirror of lean/Hex0/Rv64i.lean.
2	
3	    Same 12 instruction encodings used by bare/core.s:
4	      ADDI ADD OR SLLI LBU SB BEQ BLT BGE BGEU JAL JALR
5	    64-bit words are [Z] kept in [0, 2^64); operations wrap explicitly. Memory
6	    is byte-addressed ([Z -> Z], bytes in [0,256)). The model computes under
7	    [vm_compute] so it can be run on the real binary bytes (see Validate.v). *)
8	
9	From Coq Require Import ZArith List Lia Bool.
10	Import ListNotations.
11	Local Open Scope Z_scope.
12	
13	Definition w64 : Z := 2 ^ 64.
14	
15	Definition wrap (z : Z) : Z := z mod w64.
16	Definition wadd (a b : Z) : Z := wrap (a + b).
17	Definition wor  (a b : Z) : Z := Z.lor a b.
18	Definition wshl (a : Z) (n : Z) : Z := wrap (Z.shiftl a n).
19	
20	(* sign-extend a [k]-bit raw value to a (possibly negative) Z *)
21	Definition sext (k raw : Z) : Z :=
22	  if raw >=? 2 ^ (k - 1) then raw - 2 ^ k else raw.
23	
24	(* unsigned / signed comparisons on in-range words *)
25	Definition toS (x : Z) : Z := if x >=? 2 ^ 63 then x - w64 else x.
26	Definition ultb (a b : Z) : bool := a <? b.
27	Definition sltb (a b : Z) : bool := toS a <? toS b.
28	
29	(* extract [len] bits at offset [lo] from a 32-bit value *)
30	Definition field (w lo len : Z) : Z := (w / 2 ^ lo) mod 2 ^ len.
31	
32	Record State := mkState {
33	  reg : Z -> Z;     (* x0..x31 ; x0 forced to 0 by rget/rset *)
34	  pc  : Z;
35	  mem : Z -> Z      (* byte-addressed *)
36	}.
37	
38	Definition rget (s : State) (i : Z) : Z := if i =? 0 then 0 else s.(reg) i.
39	
40	Definition rset (s : State) (i : Z) (v : Z) : State :=
41	  if i =? 0 then s
42	  else mkState (fun j => if j =? i then v else s.(reg) j) s.(pc) s.(mem).
43	
44	Definition setPc (s : State) (p : Z) : State := mkState s.(reg) p s.(mem).
45	
46	Definition storeByte (s : State) (a b : Z) : State :=
47	  mkState s.(reg) s.(pc) (fun x => if x =? a then b mod 256 else s.(mem) x).
48	
49	Definition fetch32 (s : State) : Z :=
50	  let b0 := s.(mem) s.(pc) in
51	  let b1 := s.(mem) (s.(pc) + 1) in
52	  let b2 := s.(mem) (s.(pc) + 2) in
53	  let b3 := s.(mem) (s.(pc) + 3) in
54	  b0 + b1 * 256 + b2 * 65536 + b3 * 16777216.
55	
56	Inductive Instr :=
57	  | Iaddi (rd rs1 : Z) (imm : Z)
58	  | Iadd  (rd rs1 rs2 : Z)
59	  | Ior   (rd rs1 rs2 : Z)
60	  | Islli (rd rs1 : Z) (shamt : Z)
61	  | Ilbu  (rd rs1 : Z) (imm : Z)
62	  | Isb   (rs1 rs2 : Z) (imm : Z)
63	  | Ibeq  (rs1 rs2 : Z) (imm : Z)
64	  | Iblt  (rs1 rs2 : Z) (imm : Z)
65	  | Ibge  (rs1 rs2 : Z) (imm : Z)
66	  | Ibgeu (rs1 rs2 : Z) (imm : Z)
67	  | Ijal  (rd : Z) (imm : Z)
68	  | Ijalr (rd rs1 : Z) (imm : Z)
69	  | Iunknown.
70	
71	(* immediates are stored as sign-extended Z, ready to feed into wadd *)
72	Definition decode (w : Z) : Instr :=
73	  let opcode := field w 0 7 in
74	  let rd     := field w 7 5 in
75	  let funct3 := field w 12 3 in
76	  let rs1    := field w 15 5 in
77	  let rs2    := field w 20 5 in
78	  let funct7 := field w 25 7 in
79	  let immI   := sext 12 (field w 20 12) in
80	  let shamt  := field w 20 6 in
81	  let immS   := sext 12 (Z.lor (Z.shiftl funct7 5) rd) in
82	  let immB   := sext 13 (Z.lor (Z.lor (Z.shiftl (field w 31 1) 12) (Z.shiftl (field w 7 1) 11))
83	                               (Z.lor (Z.shiftl (field w 25 6) 5) (Z.shiftl (field w 8 4) 1))) in
84	  let immJ   := sext 21 (Z.lor (Z.lor (Z.shiftl (field w 31 1) 20) (Z.shiftl (field w 12 8) 12))
85	                               (Z.lor (Z.shiftl (field w 20 1) 11) (Z.shiftl (field w 21 10) 1))) in
86	  if opcode =? 19 then            (* 0x13 OP-IMM *)
87	    if funct3 =? 0 then Iaddi rd rs1 immI
88	    else if funct3 =? 1 then (if funct7 =? 0 then Islli rd rs1 shamt else Iunknown)
89	    else Iunknown
90	  else if opcode =? 51 then       (* 0x33 OP *)
91	    if funct7 =? 0 then
92	      (if funct3 =? 0 then Iadd rd rs1 rs2
93	       else if funct3 =? 6 then Ior rd rs1 rs2 else Iunknown)
94	    else Iunknown
95	  else if opcode =? 3 then        (* 
… [truncated 2321 chars]
```

### 🛠️ **Tool result**  ·  19:19:15; tool 11ms

```
1	/-
2	  A minimal, executable RV64I model -- exactly the 16 instruction encodings
3	  used by `bare/core.s` (hex0) and `bare/core1.s` (hex1):
4	
5	    ADDI ADD OR SLLI LBU SB BEQ BLT BGE BGEU JAL JALR   (hex0's 12)
6	    SUB SRLI LD SD                                       (added for hex1)
7	
8	  (li, mv collapse to ADDI; j = JAL x0; ret = JALR x0,ra,0; bgez/bltz are
9	  BGE/BLT vs x0). No LUI/AUIPC -- this is the whole trusted ISA surface for
10	  the hex0/hex1 rungs.
11	
12	  Words/addresses are `BitVec 64`, memory is byte-addressed (`BitVec 64 -> BitVec 8`),
13	  instructions are decoded from little-endian 32-bit words. The model is
14	  executable (`#eval`) so it can be run on the actual binary's bytes and checked
15	  against the QEMU run before any proof (see Hex0/Validate.lean).
16	-/
17	
18	namespace Rv64i
19	
20	abbrev Word := BitVec 64
21	abbrev Byte := BitVec 8
22	
23	structure State where
24	  reg : Nat → Word          -- x0..x31; x0 hardwired to 0 by rget/rset
25	  pc  : Word
26	  mem : Word → Byte
27	
28	/-- Read register `i` (x0 reads as 0). -/
29	@[inline] def State.rget (s : State) (i : Nat) : Word :=
30	  if i = 0 then 0 else s.reg i
31	
32	/-- Write register `i` (writes to x0 are ignored). -/
33	@[inline] def State.rset (s : State) (i : Nat) (v : Word) : State :=
34	  if i = 0 then s else { s with reg := fun j => if j = i then v else s.reg j }
35	
36	@[inline] def State.setPc (s : State) (p : Word) : State := { s with pc := p }
37	
38	@[inline] def State.loadByte (s : State) (a : Word) : Byte := s.mem a
39	
40	@[inline] def State.storeByte (s : State) (a : Word) (b : Byte) : State :=
41	  { s with mem := fun x => if x = a then b else s.mem x }
42	
43	/-- Fetch the little-endian 32-bit word at `pc`. -/
44	def fetch32 (s : State) : BitVec 32 :=
45	  let b0 := (s.mem s.pc).setWidth 32
46	  let b1 := (s.mem (s.pc + 1)).setWidth 32
47	  let b2 := (s.mem (s.pc + 2)).setWidth 32
48	  let b3 := (s.mem (s.pc + 3)).setWidth 32
49	  b0 ||| (b1 <<< 8) ||| (b2 <<< 16) ||| (b3 <<< 24)
50	
51	/-- Extract `len` bits starting at bit `lo` as a Nat. -/
52	@[inline] def field (w : BitVec 32) (lo len : Nat) : Nat :=
53	  (w.toNat >>> lo) &&& (2 ^ len - 1)
54	
55	inductive Instr where
56	  | addi (rd rs1 : Nat) (imm : BitVec 12)
57	  | add  (rd rs1 rs2 : Nat)
58	  | sub  (rd rs1 rs2 : Nat)
59	  | or   (rd rs1 rs2 : Nat)
60	  | slli (rd rs1 : Nat) (shamt : Nat)
61	  | srli (rd rs1 : Nat) (shamt : Nat)
62	  | lbu  (rd rs1 : Nat) (imm : BitVec 12)
63	  | ld   (rd rs1 : Nat) (imm : BitVec 12)
64	  | sb   (rs1 rs2 : Nat) (imm : BitVec 12)
65	  | sd   (rs1 rs2 : Nat) (imm : BitVec 12)
66	  | beq  (rs1 rs2 : Nat) (imm : BitVec 13)
67	  | blt  (rs1 rs2 : Nat) (imm : BitVec 13)
68	  | bge  (rs1 rs2 : Nat) (imm : BitVec 13)
69	  | bgeu (rs1 rs2 : Nat) (imm : BitVec 13)
70	  | jal  (rd : Nat) (imm : BitVec 21)
71	  | jalr (rd rs1 : Nat) (imm : BitVec 12)
72	  | unknown
73	deriving Repr, DecidableEq
74	
75	def decode (w : BitVec 32) : Instr :=
76	  let opcode := field w 0 7
77	  let rd     := field w 7 5
78	  let funct3 := field w 12 3
79	  let rs1    := field w 15 5
80	  let rs2    := field w 20 5
81	  let funct7 := field w 25 7
82	  let immI   : BitVec 12 := BitVec.ofNat 12 (field w 20 12)
83	  let shamt  := field w 20 6
84	  -- S-type immediate: [11:5]=funct7, [4:0]=rd
85	  let immS   : BitVec 12 := BitVec.ofNat 12 ((funct7 <<< 5) ||| rd)
86	  -- B-type immediate: [12]=b31 [11]=b7 [10:5]=b[30:25] [4:1]=b[11:8] [0]=0
87	  let immB   : BitVec 13 := BitVec.ofNat 13
88	      (((field w 31 1) <<< 12) ||| ((field w 7 1) <<< 11) |||
89	       ((field w 25 6) <<< 5)  ||| ((field w 8 4) <<< 1))
90	  -- J-type immediate: [20]=b31 [19:12]=b[19:12] [11]=b20 [10:1]=b[30:21] [0]=0
91	  let immJ   : BitVec 21 := BitVec.ofNat 21
92	      (((field w 31 1) <<< 20) ||| ((field w 12 8) <<< 12) |||
93	       ((field w 20 1) <<< 11) ||| ((field w 21 10) <<< 1))
94	  match opcode with
95	  | 0x13 => -- OP-IMM
96	      match funct3 with
97	      | 0x0 => .addi 
… [truncated 5109 chars]

2	
3	    Task #7 (see CROSSCHECK.md): remove "our hand-rolled RV64I model is faithful
4	    to real RISC-V" from the TCB by proving our [Rv64i.decode]/[Rv64i.step] agree
5	    with the authoritative riscv-coq semantics (coq-riscv.0.0.5, the bedrock2 /
6	    compiler model, generated from the official Haskell riscv-semantics).
7	
8	    T1 ([decode_agrees]): whenever our decoder returns one of the 12 modelled
9	    instructions, riscv-coq's [Decode.decode RV64I] returns the corresponding
10	    instruction with identical operands -- for every 32-bit word.
11	
12	    T2 ([step_agrees], forward simulation): one of our [step]s corresponds to one
13	    riscv-coq instruction cycle, preserving a state-bridge relation. *)
14	
15	From Coq Require Import ZArith List Bool Lia.
16	Import ListNotations.
17	Require Import Hex0Coq.Rv64i.
18	Require Import riscv.Spec.Decode.
19	Require Import riscv.Utility.Utility.
20	Require Import coqutil.Z.BitOps.
21	Require Import coqutil.Z.prove_Zeq_bitwise.
22	Local Open Scope Z_scope.
23	
24	(* ------------------------------------------------------------------ *)
25	(* Bridging lemmas: our field/sext primitives vs riscv-coq's          *)
26	(* bitSlice/signExtend.                                                *)
27	(* ------------------------------------------------------------------ *)
28	
29	(** Our [field w lo len] is exactly riscv-coq's [bitSlice w lo (lo+len)]. *)
30	Lemma field_bitSlice : forall w lo len,
31	    0 <= lo -> 0 <= len ->
32	    Rv64i.field w lo len = bitSlice w lo (lo + len).
33	Proof.
34	  intros w lo len Hlo Hlen.
35	  rewrite bitSlice_alt by lia.
36	  unfold bitSlice', Rv64i.field.
37	  f_equal. f_equal. lia.
38	Qed.
39	
40	(** Our [sext k raw] (case-split form) equals riscv-coq's [signExtend k]
41	    (modular form) on in-range inputs -- which bitSlice results always are. *)
42	Lemma sext_signExtend : forall k raw,
43	    1 <= k -> 0 <= raw < 2 ^ k ->
44	    Rv64i.sext k raw = signExtend k raw.
45	Proof.
46	  intros k raw Hk Hraw.
47	  unfold Rv64i.sext, signExtend.
48	  assert (Hpow : 2 ^ k = 2 * 2 ^ (k - 1)).
49	  { rewrite <- Z.pow_succ_r by lia. f_equal. lia. }
50	  assert (Hhalf_pos : 0 < 2 ^ (k - 1)) by (apply Z.pow_pos_nonneg; lia).
51	  destruct (raw >=? 2 ^ (k - 1)) eqn:E.
52	  - (* raw in [2^(k-1), 2^k): result raw - 2^k *)
53	    apply Z.geb_le in E.
54	    replace (raw + 2 ^ (k - 1)) with ((raw - 2 ^ (k - 1)) + 1 * 2 ^ k) by lia.
55	    rewrite Z.mod_add by lia.
56	    rewrite Z.mod_small by lia. lia.
57	  - (* raw in [0, 2^(k-1)): result raw *)
58	    rewrite Z.geb_leb in E. apply Z.leb_gt in E.
59	    rewrite Z.mod_small by lia. lia.
60	Qed.
61	
62	(* ------------------------------------------------------------------ *)
63	(* Range / conversion toolkit for operands.                            *)
64	(* ------------------------------------------------------------------ *)
65	
66	(** A [field] is bounded by 2^len, hence by 2^k for any k >= len. *)
67	Lemma field_range : forall w lo len, 0 <= len -> 0 <= Rv64i.field w lo len < 2 ^ len.
68	Proof. intros. unfold Rv64i.field. apply Z.mod_pos_bound. apply Z.pow_pos_nonneg; lia. Qed.
69	
70	Lemma field_lt : forall w lo len k, 0 <= len -> len <= k -> 0 <= Rv64i.field w lo len < 2 ^ k.
71	Proof.
72	  intros w lo len k Hlen Hk. pose proof (field_range w lo len Hlen) as H1.
73	  assert (2 ^ len <= 2 ^ k) by (apply Z.pow_le_mono_r; lia). lia.
74	Qed.
75	
76	(** [lor] of two k-bit values is a k-bit value. *)
77	Lemma lor_lt : forall k a b, 0 <= k -> 0 <= a < 2 ^ k -> 0 <= b < 2 ^ k -> 0 <= Z.lor a b < 2 ^ k.
78	Proof.
79	  intros k a b Hk Ha Hb. split.
80	  - apply Z.lor_nonneg; lia.
81	  - assert (Z.shiftr (Z.lor a b) k = 0) as Hs.
82	    { rewrite Z.shiftr_lor.

84	      rewrite (Z.div_small a) by lia. rewrite (Z.div_small b) by lia. apply Z.lor_0_l. }
85	    rewrite Z.shiftr_d

1	(** * RvCrossRun.v -- the transport corollary [core_refines_riscv] (task #7, T2).
2	
3	    [step_agrees] (RvCrossExec.v) shows ONE [Rv64i.step] = ONE riscv-coq
4	    [Run.run1 RV64I] cycle, under the state bridge [Rrel] and the per-step side
5	    conditions [WFstep].  This file lifts that single-step simulation over a WHOLE
6	    run by induction (the analogue of [loop_correct]) and composes it with the
7	    finished [core_refines]:
8	
9	      - [rrun]          -- iterate [run1] in lockstep with our [runUntil], stopping
10	                           when the model halts ([pc = 0]).
11	      - [transport_run] -- forward simulation: given [Rrel] at the start and the
12	                           per-step side conditions along the run ([RunWF]), [rrun]
13	                           succeeds and lands [Rrel]-related to [runUntil].
14	      - [core_refines_riscv] -- instantiate at [mkInit]; compose with the model
15	                           result ([init_loopinv] + [loop_correct], i.e. exactly the
16	                           first half of [core_refines]) so the RISC-V REFERENCE
17	                           MODEL running the real [core] bytes computes [coreSpec]
18	                           (halts with the spec status in a0, length in a1, and a
19	                           state [Rrel]-related to the spec output in memory).
20	
21	    What remains as explicit hypotheses (the honest residual, factored cleanly):
22	      1. [Rrel (mkInit ...) m D] -- a riscv-coq init machine matching our init.
23	      2. [RunWF ...] -- the §5 side conditions (fetch executable + mapped, branch/
24	         jump targets 4-aligned, load/store targets in [D], decode <> Iunknown) hold
25	         at every non-halted state along the run.  These are the per-cycle
26	         obligations that [step_agrees] consumes; discharging them unconditionally
27	         from the [CodeLoaded]/[LoopInv] geometry (xaddr preservation, store
28	         disjointness) is a separate, larger effort -- see CROSSCHECK.md §3/§5. *)
29	
30	From Coq Require Import ZArith List Lia Bool. Import ListNotations.
31	Require Import Hex0Coq.Rv64i Hex0Coq.RvCross Hex0Coq.RvCrossStep Hex0Coq.RvCrossExec.
32	Require Import Hex0Coq.Spec Hex0Coq.Image Hex0Coq.Harness Hex0Coq.Refine.
33	Require Import riscv.Spec.Decode riscv.Spec.Machine riscv.Platform.Run.

35	Require Import riscv.Utility.Monads. Import OStateOperations.
36	Require Import coqutil.Word.Interface coqutil.Word.Properties coqutil.Word.Bitwidth.
37	Require Import coqutil.Map.Interface coqutil.Map.Properties coqutil.Byte.
38	Local Open Scope Z_scope.
39	
40	(* iterate [Rv64i.step] [k] times, with NO halt check -- so the index shift
41	   [nstep (S k) s = nstep k (step s)] holds DEFINITIONALLY (the lemma below relies
42	   on it).  This is the trace of model states a run visits before it halts. *)
43	Fixpoint nstep (k : nat) (s : Rv64i.State) : Rv64i.State :=
44	  match k with
45	  | O => s
46	  | S j => nstep j (Rv64i.step s)
47	  end.
48	
49	Section Run.
50	  Context {BW: Bitwidth 64}.
51	  Context {word: word.word 64} {word_ok: word.ok word}.
52	  Context {Mem: map.map word Init.Byte.byte} {Mem_ok: map.ok Mem}.
53	  Context {Registers: map.map Z word} {Reg_ok: map.ok Registers}.
54	
55	  Notation RMach := (@RiscvMachine.RiscvMachine 64 word Registers Mem).
56	
57	  (* run [run1] in lockstep with [runUntil 0 _ s]: at each cycle, if the model has
58	     halted ([pc = 0]) stop and return the current machine; otherwise take one
59	     [run1] cycle (which must succeed) and recurse on [step s]. *)
60	  Fixpoint rrun (fuel : nat) (s : Rv64i.State) (m : RMach) : option RMach :=
61	    match fuel with
62	    | O => Some m
63	    | S k => if s.(Rv64i.pc) =? 0 then Some m
64	             else match Run.run1 RV64I m with
65	                  | (Some tt, m') => rrun k (Rv64i.step s) m'
66	                  | _ => None
67	                  end
68	    end.

(** * General refinement (T1) in Coq -- mirror of lean/Hex0/Refine.lean.

    Proof-grade theorem: for ALL inputs, the real `core` computes `coreSpec`.
    No vm_compute on the general statement -- it is genuine induction.

    STATUS: `core_refines` is FULLY PROVED, `Admitted`-free.  `loop_iteration`
    (the per-token dispatch) is now discharged via the head-char case analysis
    (spacing/byte/comment + the four halting error classes), each branch a
    proved lemma.  `Print Assumptions core_refines` reports ONLY the standard
    `functional_extensionality_dep` axiom (used for `mem : Z -> Z` state
    equality) -- no `loop_iteration`, no `sorry`/`admit`.  Everything below is
    kernel-checked, mirroring `lean/Hex0/Refine.lean` §5:
      - `fetch_code` + all 12 `step_*` lemmas + state/storeByte projections
        (`decode (wordAt off)` reduces under `vm_compute` at concrete offsets, so
        the step lemmas apply exactly as in Lean);
      - arithmetic toolkit: `wrap_small`, `wadd_id`, `toS_small`, `sltb_small`;
      - `runUntil` composition: `runUntil_halt`, `runUntil_one`, `runUntil_S`,
        `runUntil_add`, `runUntil_stab` (large-fuel halt absorption);
      - spec-side token decomposition: `decodeS_spacing`/`byte`/`comment`;
      - `core_eof` -- the EOF base case (4-step run to a correct halt);
      - `LoopInv` (the 18-field invariant) + `eof_result`;
      - `loop_correct` -- the induction (fuel bound `50*|rest| + 4`);
      - `init_loopinv` -- the prologue (2-step run to the loop head);
      - `core_refines` -- prologue + induction + `runOn<->coreSpec` conversion.
    The per-token tail (spacing/byte/comment + the four halting error classes,
    the ~2500 Lean lines) is now fully ported and assembled by `loop_iteration`.
    Each branch lemma carries an explicit fuel bound (`k <= 50*(chars consumed)`)
    so the fixed-fuel `runOn` (100000) absorbs the run via `runUntil_stab`.
    Two Coq-specific notes vs Lean (see PROOF.md §8): (1) `runOn` uses a *fixed*
    fuel (100000), so the assembly bounds the step count (Lean used ∃fuel) and
    absorbs the slack via `runUntil_stab` -- note `lia` cannot reason about the
    nat literal `100000` (it is `Nat.of_num_uint`), so the bound `F <= 100000`
    is proved through `Z` (`Nat2Z.inj_le` + `vm_compute (Z.of_nat 100000)`);
    (2) the model's bytes are `Z` but the spec is on `nat`, so `LoopInv`/dispatch
    carry `Z.of_nat`/`Z.to_nat` (`zin`) conversions. *)

From Coq Require Import ZArith List Lia Bool.
From Equations Require Import Equations.
From Hex0Coq Require Import Spec Rv64i Image Harness.
Import ListNotations.
Local Open Scope Z_scope.

(** ** Per-step reduction primitive (PROVED).
    `core`'s first instruction `li t0,0` = `addi x5,x0,0`, bytes 93 02 00 00,
    word 0x293 = 659. One [step] computes its effect; data stays symbolic. *)
Theorem step_li_t0 : forall s,
  s.(mem) s.(pc) = 147 ->
  s.(mem) (s.(pc) + 1) = 2 ->
  s.(mem) (s.(pc) + 2) = 0 ->
  s.(mem) (s.(pc) + 3) = 0 ->
  s.(pc) = 2147483784 ->
  (step s).(pc) = 2147483788 /\ rget (step s) 5 = 0.
Proof.
  intros s h0 h1 h2 h3 hpc.
  unfold step, fetch32.
  rewrite h0, h1, h2, h3.
  (* fetched word is now the closed value 659; decode + effect compute *)
  change (147 + 2 * 256 + 0 * 65536 + 0 * 16777216) with 659.
  rewrite hpc. cbn. split; reflexivity.
Qed.

  Definition loadN(n: nat)(kind: SourceType)(a: word): OState RiscvMachine (HList.tuple byte n) :=
    mach <- get;
    v <- fail_if_None (Memory.load_bytes n mach.(getMem) a);
    match kind with
    | Fetch => if isXAddr4B a mach.(getXAddrs) then Return v else fail_hard

  Definition storeN(n: nat)(kind: SourceType)(a: word)(v: HList.tuple byte n) :=
    mach <- get;
    m <- fail_if_None (Memory.store_bytes n mach.(getMem) a v);

    Lemma unsigned_slu_shamtZ: forall (x: word) (a: Z),
        0 <= a < width ->
        word.unsigned (word.slu x (word.of_Z a)) = word.wrap (Z.shiftl (word.unsigned x) a).
    Proof.
      intros. assert (width <= 2 ^ width) by (apply Zpow_facts.Zpower2_le_lin; blia).
      rewrite word.unsigned_slu; rewrite word.unsigned_of_Z; unfold word.wrap; rewrite (Z.mod_small a); blia.
    Qed.

    Lemma unsigned_sru_shamtZ: forall (x: word) (a: Z),
        0 <= a < width ->
        word.unsigned (word.sru x (word.of_Z a)) = Z.shiftr (word.unsigned x) a.

      intros. assert (width <= 2 ^ width) by (apply Zpow_facts.Zpower2_le_lin; blia).
      rewrite word.unsigned_sru_nowrap; rewrite word.unsigned_of_Z;
        unfold word.wrap; rewrite (Z.mod_small a); blia.

Qed.


(** ** signExtend *)

Definition signExtend(oldwidth: Z)(z: Z): Z :=
  (z + 2^(oldwidth-1)) mod 2^oldwidth - 2^(oldwidth-1).

Definition signExtend_bitwise(width n: Z): Z :=
  if Z.testbit n (width - 1)
  then (Z.lor (Z.land n (Z.ones width)) (Z.shiftl (-1) width))
  else (Z.land n (Z.ones width)).
```

### 🛠️ **Tool result**  ·  19:32:38; tool 83ms

```
Require Import Coq.ZArith.ZArith.
Require Import coqutil.Z.Lia.
Require Import coqutil.Datatypes.HList coqutil.Datatypes.PrimitivePair.
Require Import coqutil.Z.bitblast.
Require Import coqutil.Z.prove_Zeq_bitwise.
Require Import coqutil.Byte.
Local Set Universe Polymorphism.

Local Open Scope Z_scope.

Section LittleEndian. Local Set Default Proof Using "All".

  Fixpoint combine_deprecated (n : nat) : forall (bs : tuple byte n), Z :=
    match n with
    | O => fun _ => 0
    | S n => fun bs => Z.lor (byte.unsigned (pair._1 bs))
                             (Z.shiftl (combine_deprecated n (pair._2 bs)) 8)
    end.
  Notation combine := combine_deprecated (only parsing).

  Fixpoint split_deprecated (n : nat) (w : Z) : tuple byte n :=
    match n with
    | O => tt
    | S n => pair.mk (byte.of_Z w) (split_deprecated n (Z.shiftr w 8))
    end.
  Notation split := split_deprecated (only parsing).

  Lemma combine_split (n : nat) (z : Z) :
    combine_deprecated n (split_deprecated n z) = z mod 2 ^ (Z.of_nat n * 8).
  Proof.
    revert z; induction n.
    - cbn. intros. rewrite Z.mod_1_r. trivial.
    - cbn [split_deprecated combine_deprecated PrimitivePair.pair._1 PrimitivePair.pair._2]; intros.
      erewrite IHn; clear IHn.
      rewrite byte.unsigned_of_Z, Nat2Z.inj_succ, Z.mul_succ_l by blia.
      unfold byte.wrap.
      rewrite <-! Z.land_ones by blia.
      Z.bitblast.
  Qed.

  Lemma split_combine (n: nat) bs :
    split_deprecated n (combine_deprecated n bs) = bs.
  Proof.
    revert bs; induction n.
    - destruct bs. reflexivity.
    - destruct bs; cbn [split_deprecated combine_deprecated PrimitivePair.pair._1 PrimitivePair.pair._2]; intros.
      specialize (IHn _2).
      f_equal.
      { eapply byte.unsigned_inj.
        rewrite byte.unsigned_of_Z, <-byte.wrap_unsigned; cbv [byte.wrap].
        Z.bitblast; cbn; subst.
        rewrite (Z.testbit_neg_r _ (i-8)) by blia.
        Z.bitblast_core. }
      { rewrite <-IHn.
        rewrite combine_split.
        f_equal.
        rewrite <-byte.wrap_unsigned; cbv [byte.wrap].
        Z.bitblast; subst; cbn.
        rewrite <-IHn.
        rewrite combine_split.
```

  (** connection to the model state: 8 in-domain data bytes at [of_Z az]
      load successfully and combine to [Rv64i.loadWord s az]. *)
  Lemma load8_conn : forall s (m:RMach) D az,
    Rrel s m D -> 0 <= az -> az + 8 <= 2 ^ 64 ->
    (forall i, 0 <= i < 8 -> D (word.add (word.of_Z az) (word.of_Z i))) ->
    exists bs, Memory.load_bytes 8 m.(getMem) (word.of_Z az) = Some bs /\
               LittleEndian.combine 8 bs = Rv64i.loadWord s az /\
               0 <= Rv64i.loadWord s az < 2 ^ 64.
  Proof.
    intros s m D az HR Haz0 Hnw HD.
    destruct HR as (HRA & HMA & HPA).
    assert (Hai : forall i, 0 <= i < 8 ->
              word.unsigned (word.add (word.of_Z az) (word.of_Z i)) = az + i)
      by (intros; ZnWords).
    assert (Hgi : forall i, 0 <= i < 8 ->
              map.get m.(getMem) (word.add (word.of_Z az) (word.of_Z i))
                = Some (byte.of_Z (s.(mem) (az + i)))).

      rewrite (Hai i Hi) in Hg. exact Hg. }
    assert (Hri : forall i, 0 <= i < 8 -> 0 <= s.(mem) (az + i) < 256).

      rewrite (Hai i Hi) in Hr. exact Hr. }

/-
  Shared harness for running the real hex1 binary image through the model:
  loading bytes into memory, building an initial state, reading the output
  region. Used by Hex1/Validate.lean (executable diff-test) and
  Hex1/Certify.lean (native-checked certification theorems).

  Reuses Hex0's `Rv64i.Harness.loadBytes`/`readMem`; only `initOn` differs:
  core1 additionally takes a4 = label-table scratch (reg 14).
-/
import Hex0.Harness
import Hex1.Image
open Rv64i

namespace Rv64i.Harness1

/-- Initial machine state for core1: code + `inp` loaded, registers set per
    the calling convention (a0=in_ptr, a1=in_len, a2=out_ptr, a3=cap,
    a4=lbl_ptr, ra=0 sentinel), pc = core1 entry. The label table is NOT
    pre-initialized (core1 initializes it itself). -/
def initOn (inp : List Nat) (cap : Nat) : State :=
  { pc  := BitVec.ofNat 64 Image1.coreAddr
    mem := Harness.loadBytes Image1.inputAddr inp
             (Harness.loadBytes Image1.coreAddr Image1.coreBytes (fun _ => 0))
    reg := fun i =>
      if i = 1 then 0
      else if i = 10 then BitVec.ofNat 64 Image1.inputAddr
      else if i = 11 then BitVec.ofNat 64 inp.length
      else if i = 12 then BitVec.ofNat 64 Image1.outAddr
      else if i = 13 then BitVec.ofNat 64 cap
      else if i = 14 then BitVec.ofNat 64 Image1.lblAddr
      else 0 }

/-- Observable result of running the real core1 on `inp` with capacity `cap`,
    using `fuel` steps: (status, output bytes, out_len). -/
def observe (inp : List Nat) (cap fuel : Nat) : Nat × List Nat × Nat :=
  let f := runFuel 0 fuel (initOn inp cap)
  ((f.rget 10).toNat, Harness.readMem f.mem Image1.outAddr (f.rget 11).toNat,
   (f.rget 11).toNat)

end Rv64i.Harness1
```

### 🛠️ **Tool result**  ·  19:53:20; tool 103ms

```
  fun x => if x =? l then Some pos else lab x.

(* Decoder state: expecting a high nibble / a low nibble (after high [hi]) /
   the label byte of a ':' definition / the label byte of a '%' reference. *)
Inductive St1 := High1 | Low1 (hi:nat) | Col1 | Pct1.

(* Phase 1 (scan): tokenize, collect label positions, track the virtual
   output position. Returns (labels, m, status); [m] is the output position
   reached when the scan stops (the error site's position, or the total).
   Mirrors [scan] in hex1.c statement-for-statement. *)
Equations? scan1 (s:St1) (lab:Labels) (pos:nat) (l:list nat)
    : (Labels * nat * Status1) by wf (length l) lt :=
  scan1 High1 lab pos [] := (lab, pos, Ok1);
  scan1 (Low1 _) lab pos [] := (lab, pos, Trailing1);
  scan1 Col1 lab pos [] := (lab, pos, TrailTok1);
  scan1 Pct1 lab pos [] := (lab, pos, TrailTok1);
  scan1 High1 lab pos (c :: rest) :=
    if isComment c then scan1 High1 lab pos (skipComment rest)
    else if isSpace c then scan1 High1 lab pos rest
    else if c =? c_colon then scan1 Col1 lab pos rest
    else if c =? c_pct then scan1 Pct1 lab pos rest
    else match nibble c with
         | None => (lab, pos, Unknown1)
         | Some hi => scan1 (Low1 hi) lab pos rest
         end;
  scan1 (Low1 _) lab pos (c :: rest) :=
    if isLowStop1 c then (lab, pos, Split1)
    else match nibble c with
         | None => (lab, pos, Unknown1)
         | Some _ => scan1 High1 lab (pos + 1) rest
         end;
  scan1 Col1 lab pos (lc :: rest) :=
    match lab lc with
    | Some _ => (lab, pos, Dup1)
    | None => scan1 High1 (setLabel lab lc pos) pos rest
    end;
  scan1 Pct1 lab pos (_ :: rest) := scan1 High1 lab (pos + 4) rest.
Proof.
  all: cbn [length]; try lia.
  all: match goal with
       | [ |- context[length (skipComment ?l)] ] =>
           pose proof (skipComment_len l); cbn [length]; lia
       end.
Qed.

(* The 4 little-endian bytes of the i32 relative offset [p - (pos + 4)]
   (label position [p], field position [pos]), reduced mod 2^32 (two's
   complement truncation; exact for outputs < 2 GiB). *)
Definition offWord (p pos : nat) : nat :=
  Z.to_nat (((Z.of_nat p - (Z.of_nat pos + 4)) mod (2^32))%Z).
Definition offBytes (p pos : nat) : list nat :=
  let off := offWord p pos in
  [off mod 256; off / 2^8 mod 256; off / 2^16 mod 256; off / 2^24 mod 256].

(* Nat division/mod by large literals must never be unfolded by simpl/cbn:
   Nat.divmod recurses on the literal (2^24 deep) and overflows the stack. *)
Global Arguments offWord : simpl never.
Global Arguments offBytes : simpl never.

(* Phase 2 (emit): emit bytes and resolve references against the collected
   label map. Total (defined on all inputs); under a clean scan the only
   reachable stop is [Undef1] (or [Ok1] at EOF). [pos] is the output
   position = length of output emitted so far. Mirrors [emit] in hex1.c. *)
(* Phase-2 helpers: cons/append onto the first component of a result pair.
   (Equations' derivation stack-overflows on let-'(a,b) destructuring of the
   recursive call here; fst/snd projections elaborate fine and are
   definitionally equal.) *)
Definition consOut (b:nat) (r:list nat * Status1) : list nat * Status1 :=
  (b :: fst r, snd r).
Definition appOut (bs:list nat) (r:list nat * Status1) : list nat * Status1 :=

  emit1 High1 lab pos (c :: rest) :=
    if isComment c then emit1 High1 lab pos (skipComment rest)
    else if isSpace c then emit1 High1 lab pos rest
    else if c =? c_colon then emit1 Col1 lab pos rest
    else if c =? c_pct then emit1 Pct1 lab pos rest

### 🛠️ **Tool result**  ·  20:32:30; tool 75ms

```
---
name: coq-equations-gotchas
description: Coq 8.20 Equations stack overflows — let-pattern destructuring and simpl on Nat division by big literals
metadata: 
  node_type: memory
  type: reference
  originSessionId: c56c2984-d7d8-4037-8d21-eb3534083b57
---

Two stack-overflow traps hit while porting hex1 specs to Coq (2026-06-04), both manifest as `Error: Stack overflow` with no other diagnostics:

1. **Equations + `let '(a,b) := f rec_call in ...`**: an `Equations ... by wf` definition whose rhs destructures the recursive call with a let-pattern can blow the OCaml stack during Equations' post-Qed processing (emit1 died; oddly decodeS/lexF with one such pattern were fine). Fix: route through tiny helper defs (`consOut b r := (b :: fst r, snd r)`, `appOut`), definitionally equal.

2. **`simpl`/`cbn` on Nat `/`,`mod` by large literals**: `off / 2^16 mod 256` — simpl unfolds `Nat.divmod`, which recurses on the 16M literal. Fix at the definition site: `Global Arguments offWord : simpl never.` / same for offBytes. Also avoid blanket `simpl` over goals containing Equations-compiled WF functions — use `cbn [theFixpoint]` whitelists.

Also: `simp f` (Equations rewrite db) rewrites EXHAUSTIVELY — after conditions are rewritten it may step through several states at once; don't script a second `simp f` expecting one-step behavior ("No such goal" errors follow). Related: [[coq-build-env]].
---
name: hex1-campaign-frontier
description: "hex1 — Lean Refine1 COMPLETE (core1_refines proved, lake build green); remaining frontier is the Coq side (Rv64i.v extension + cross-check + Refine1.v port)"
metadata: 
  node_type: memory
  type: project
  originSessionId: c56c2984-d7d8-4037-8d21-eb3534083b57
---

hex1 status (2026-06-04): program (HEX1.md/hex1.c/bare/core1.s), 22k fuzz, Lean+Coq spec/grammar proofs, native_decide certification, AND the Lean general refinement are ALL DONE. `core1_refines` in lean/Hex1/Refine.lean (~9000 lines, sorry-free, no native_decide) proved chunk-by-chunk (chunks 1-17, each committed); `import Hex1.Refine` is in Hex1.lean and full `lake build` is green — the [[lean-build-root-gotcha]] no longer applies to Refine.lean.

**Why:** multi-session proof campaign; don't re-derive what's proved — the only remaining hex1 work is the Coq side.

**How to apply:** Read REFINE1.md (lemma map + proof-style gotchas) and RESUME-HEX1.md before touching the files. Remaining work (RESUME-HEX1.md "Task list state"): extend coq/Rv64i.v (+sub/srli/ld/sd — BREAKS RvCross.v embed: extend embed, decode_agrees, step_agrees with an 8-byte memory bridge for ld/sd reusing RvCrossStep.v's fetch32 machinery), then Harness1.v/Certify1.v (vm_compute), then a Refine1.v port; finally a hex1 section in TCB.md. Mind [[isa-surface-discipline]], [[coq-equations-gotchas]], [[commit-intermediate-checkpoints]]; related [[task7-crosscheck-frontier]].
```

1	# Trusted Computing Base (hex0 rung)

6	## Proven (NOT in the TCB)
7	
8	- **The `decode` spec** (`coq/Spec.v`, `lean/Hex0/Spec.lean`) — the meaning of
9	  hex0. The two definitions compute identically on a battery of inputs, and the
10	  Lean `decodeS` is **proved equivalent to the published BNF grammar of HEX0.md**
11	  (`lean/Hex0/Grammar.lean`): `decodeS .High inp = (out,st) ↔ Parse inp out st`,
12	  with the grammar shown total (`parse_total`) and deterministic (`parse_det`) —
13	  every input is *either* a valid program (→ `Ok`) *or* exactly one error class,
14	  and the classification matches the spec.
15	- **The RV64I model** (`*/Rv64i.*`) executes the *actual* `core` bytes and
16	  matches `coreSpec` (differential battery + the embedded input).
17	- **Concrete certification** (`*/Certify.*`) — the deployed bytes equal
18	  `coreSpec` on the embedded input and every error class. *Finite/testing-grade.*
19	- **General refinement** (`lean/Hex0/Refine.lean`) — `core_refines : ∀ inp cap,
20	  WellFormed inp cap → ∃ fuel, observe inp cap fuel = coreSpec inp cap`. **Fully
21	  proved, `sorry`-free** (axioms: `propext`/`Quot.sound` — `Classical.choice`-free).
22	  The **Coq `Refine.v`** port now proves `core_refines` **fully, `Admitted`-free**
23	  (`Print Assumptions core_refines` ⇒ only `functional_extensionality_dep`, a
24	  standard consistent axiom for `mem : Z → Z` state equality). Everything

### 🛠️ **Tool result**  ·  20:34:29; tool 91ms

```
# CROSSCHECK — ISA model vs. an authoritative RISC-V spec (task #7)

This is the plan for the **last open item** in the hex0 verification tower: removing
*"our hand-rolled RV64I model is faithful to real RISC-V"* from the TCB
(`TCB.md` item 1) by cross-checking `Rv64i.{v,lean}`'s decode+step against an
authoritative, independently-maintained RISC-V semantics.

Read with `STATUS.md` (state), `TCB.md` (trust boundary), `PROOF.md` (refinement
methodology). Everything *above* the ISA layer (`core_refines`, grammar,
certification) is already proved in both Lean and Coq; this is the floor of the
tower.

---

## 0. Status of this task after recon (2026-06-02)

**The oracle is already installed and the cross-check empirically holds on the
real binary.** Concretely:

- The opam switch (`~/.opam/CP.2025.01.0~8.20~2025.01`) ships **`coq-riscv.0.0.5`**
  (the MIT **riscv-coq** / *riscv-semantics* model — the spec used by
  bedrock2/`compiler`, generated by `hs-to-coq` from the official Haskell
  `riscv-semantics`) plus its deps **`coq-coqutil.0.0.6`** (`word`, `map`).
  Path: `~/.opam/.../lib/coq/user-contrib/riscv/` (on Coq's default load path —
  `Require Import riscv.Spec.Decode.` just works; verified).
- All **12** instruction forms `core` uses exist in riscv-coq's `InstructionI`
  (`Addi Add Or Slli Lbu Sb Beq Blt Bge Bgeu Jal Jalr`).
- **Empirical differential already run and PASSED** (`/tmp/cross_diff.v`, reproduced
  below): decoding every one of the **81** instruction words of the real `core`
  image both ways agrees **field-for-field** (opcode, rd/rs1/rs2, every immediate),
  and our model decodes **0** of them to `Iunknown`. So on the actual deployed
  bytes, our decoder = riscv-coq's decoder, exactly.

  ```
  Eval vm_compute in (allAgree 81).   (* = true  *)
  Eval vm_compute in (cntUnknown 81). (* = 0     *)
  ```

What remains is to turn that empirical agreement into **theorems** (general over
all 32-bit words for decode; over the 12 forms under a state-bridge for execute),
which is what actually discharges the TCB obligation.

### ✅ T1 is DONE (`coq/RvCross.v`, 2026-06-02)

`decode_agrees` is **proved, `Admitted`-free, and closed under the global context
(ZERO axioms)** — kernel-checked, built by `make` in the pipeline:

```coq
Theorem decode_agrees : forall w, 0 <= w < 2 ^ 32 ->
  forall i, Rv64i.decode w = i -> i <> Iunknown -> Decode.decode RV64I w = embed i.
```

`Print Assumptions decode_agrees` ⇒ *Closed under the global context*. So for **every**
32-bit word, whenever our decoder yields one of the 12 modelled instructions,
riscv-coq's `decode RV64I` yields the corresponding instruction with identical
operands. **Our decoder is no longer trusted — it is proved equal to the reference
decoder.** Proof structure actually used (≈300 lines):
- bridges `field_bitSlice` (`field = bitSlice`), `sext_signExtend` (on in-range inputs);
- range toolkit `field_lt`/`lor_lt`/`shiftl_field_lt` + `range_tac` (immediate bounds),
  `field_sub0` (subfield-of-zero, for SLLI's funct6/shamtHi from funct7=0);
```

===

> Our decode (all 32-bit words, modulo the SLLI `shamt<32` subset) and our step
> (the 12 forms, for 4-aligned targets / mapped+executable memory — all true of
> the loaded `core`) **agree with riscv-coq** (`coq-riscv.0.0.5`), the
> bedrock2/`compiler` RISC-V semantics. Residual trust: that **riscv-coq itself**
> faithfully models the ISA — a far larger, externally-audited, widely-used
> artifact than our 136-line model.

i.e. we trade "trust our tiny bespoke model" for "trust the community's reference
model", which is the standard and much stronger position.

## 9. Effort & sequencing

- **T1 (decode_agrees)**: ~150–250 lines, self-contained, no monad/coqutil. **Do first.**
  High value (covers *all* inputs), low risk — the empirical probe already shows the
  goal is true.
- **T2 (step_agrees)**: ~300–500 lines; the new machinery is the `coqutil`
  `word`/`map` bridge and the `OState` unfolding. Build the bridge lemmas
  (`word_bridge`, `reg_bridge`, `mem_bridge`, `combine_fetch`) once, then the 12
  `exec_*` are mechanical.

Suggested commits: (1) `RvCross.v` skeleton + `embed` + empirical `Example`;
(2) `field_range`/`imm_eq` + `decode_agrees` (T1 done); (3) coqutil bridge lemmas;
(4) `exec_*` per group; (5) `step_agrees` (T2 done); (6) update `STATUS.md`/`TCB.md`.

## 10. Open questions to confirm during implementation

- **`translate` on Minimal** reduces to identity for size-1 (and size-4 fetch)?
  Read `Spec.Machine.translate`'s Minimal binding; if it alignment-checks, fold the
  (trivial, size-1) obligation into `WF`. *(Most likely a no-op `Return a`.)*
- **`OState` definition / `Bind` reduction** — confirm `Platform.Minimal` uses
  `coqutil`'s `OState` (state→(option A × state)) and that `run1` reduces cleanly
  under `simpl`/`cbn` (it should; `Run.run1` is short).
- **`reg_eqb` vs `Z.eqb`-on-unsigned** for `Beq` — confirm `word.eqb`/`reg_eqb` is
  decidable equality on `word`, equal to `Z.eqb` on `unsigned` (coqutil
  `word.eqb_true/false` + injectivity of `unsigned` on canonical `Naive` words).
- Whether to also state the **reverse decode direction** (riscv `IInstruction` ⇒ our
  non-`Iunknown`) for the 6 opcodes we model — nice-to-have completeness, not needed
  for the TCB claim.
```

60	Qed.
61	
62	(** ** Engine: fetch at a code offset + per-instruction step lemmas.
63	    Mirror of `Refine.lean`'s `fetch_code` + `step_*`. Words are [Z]; the
64	    decode of a closed word reduces under [cbn]/[vm_compute] at call sites. *)
65	
66	Definition nthb (i : Z) : Z := nth (Z.to_nat i) coreBytes 0.
67	
68	Definition wordAt (off : Z) : Z :=
69	  nthb off + nthb (off + 1) * 256 + nthb (off + 2) * 65536 + nthb (off + 3) * 16777216.
70	
71	Definition CodeLoaded (s : State) : Prop :=
72	  forall i, 0 <= i < Z.of_nat (length coreBytes) -> s.(mem) (coreAddr + i) = nthb i.
73	
74	(* state projections *)
75	Lemma setPc_pc s p : (setPc s p).(pc) = p. Proof. reflexivity. Qed.
76	Lemma setPc_mem s p : (setPc s p).(mem) = s.(mem). Proof. reflexivity. Qed.
77	Lemma setPc_rget s p i : rget (setPc s p) i = rget s i. Proof. reflexivity. Qed.
78	Lemma rset_pc s rd v : (rset s rd v).(pc) = s.(pc).
79	Proof. unfold rset; destruct (rd =? 0); reflexivity. Qed.
80	Lemma rset_mem s rd v : (rset s rd v).(mem) = s.(mem).
81	Proof. unfold rset; destruct (rd =? 0); reflexivity. Qed.
82	Lemma rget_zero s : rget s 0 = 0. Proof. reflexivity. Qed.
83	
84	Lemma rset_rget s rd v i : rd <> 0 -> i <> 0 ->
85	  rget (rset s rd v) i = if i =? rd then v else rget s i.
86	Proof.
87	  intros hrd hi. unfold rget, rset.
88	  destruct (rd =? 0) eqn:Erd; [apply Z.eqb_eq in Erd; lia|].
89	  destruct (i =? 0) eqn:Ei; [apply Z.eqb_eq in Ei; lia|].
90	  reflexivity.
91	Qed.
92	
93	Lemma fetch_code : forall s off,
94	  CodeLoaded s -> 0 <= off -> off + 3 < Z.of_nat (length coreBytes) ->
95	  s.(pc) = coreAddr + off -> fetch32 s = wordAt off.
96	Proof.
97	  intros s off hc ho1 ho2 hpc.
98	  unfold fetch32, wordAt. rewrite hpc.
99	  replace (coreAddr + off + 1) with (coreAddr + (off + 1)) by lia.
100	  replace (coreAddr + off + 2) with (coreAddr + (off + 2)) by lia.
101	  replace (coreAddr + off + 3) with (coreAddr + (off + 3)) by lia.
102	  rewrite (hc off ltac:(lia)), (hc (off+1) ltac:(lia)),
103	          (hc (off+2) ltac:(lia)), (hc (off+3) ltac:(lia)).
104	  reflexivity.
105	Qed.
106	
107	Lemma step_addi : forall s off rd rs1 imm,
108	  CodeLoaded s -> 0 <= off -> off + 3 < Z.of_nat (length coreBytes) ->
109	  s.(pc) = coreAddr + off -> decode (wordAt off) = Iaddi rd rs1 imm ->
110	  step s = setPc (rset s rd (wadd (rget s rs1) imm)) (wadd s.(pc) 4).
111	Proof.
112	  intros s off rd rs1 imm hc ho1 ho2 hpc hd.
113	  unfold step. rewrite (fetch_code s off hc ho1 ho2 hpc), hd. reflexivity.
114	Qed.
115	
116	Lemma step_bgeu : forall s off rs1 rs2 imm,
117	  CodeLoaded s -> 0 <= off -> off + 3 < Z.of_nat (length coreBytes) ->
118	  s.(pc) = coreAddr + off -> decode (wordAt off) = Ibgeu rs1 rs2 imm ->
119	  step s = setPc s (if ultb (rget s rs1) (rget s rs2) then wadd s.(pc) 4 else wadd s.(pc) imm).
120	Proof.
121	  intros s off rs1 rs2 imm hc ho1 ho2 hpc hd.
122	  unfold step. rewrite (fetch_code s off hc ho1 ho2 hpc), hd. reflexivity.
123	Qed.
124	
125	Lemma step_add : forall s off rd rs1 rs2,
126	  CodeLoaded s -> 0 <= off -> off + 3 < Z.of_nat (length coreBytes) ->
127	  s.(pc) = coreAddr + off -> decode (wordAt off) = Iadd rd rs1 rs2 ->
128	  step s = setPc (rset s rd (wadd (rget s rs1) (rget s rs2))) (wadd s.(pc) 4).
129	Proof. intros s off rd rs1 rs2 hc ho1 ho2 hpc hd.
130	  unfold step. rewrite (fetch_code s off hc ho1 ho2 hpc), hd. reflexivity. Qed.

132	Lemma step_or : forall s off rd rs1 rs2,
133	  CodeLoaded s -> 0 <= off -> off + 3 < Z.of_nat (length coreBytes) ->
134	  s.(pc) = coreAddr + off -> decode (wordAt off) = Ior rd rs1 rs2 ->
135	  step s = setPc (rset s rd (wor (rget s rs1) (rget s rs2))) (wadd s.(pc) 4).
136	Proof. intros s off rd rs1 rs2 hc ho1 ho2 hpc hd.

438	  CodeLoaded s -> 0 <= off -> off + 4 + 3 < Z.of_nat (length coreBytes) ->
439	  s.(pc) = coreAddr + off ->

### 🛠️ **Tool result**  ·  20:43:33; tool 86ms

```
(* the sign test [bge slot,x0]: an undefined slot is negative ... *)
Lemma encodeSlot_none_neg : sltb (encodeSlot None) 0 = true.
Proof. reflexivity. Qed.

(* ... and a defined slot (position < 2^63) is non-negative. *)
Lemma encodeSlot_some_nonneg p : Z.of_nat p < 2 ^ 63 ->
  sltb (encodeSlot (Some p)) 0 = false.
Proof.
  intros hp. cbn. rewrite (sltb_small _ _ ltac:(lia) ltac:(lia)).
  apply Z.ltb_ge. lia.
Qed.

(** ** Slot addressing and table access. *)

(* slli t3,t2,3 on a byte value: the slot offset 8c *)
```

### 🛠️ **Tool result**  ·  20:47:30; tool 80ms

```
Qed.

(* the init loop runs to completion: 3*(256-j) steps to pass-1 entry *)
Lemma init_loop : forall inp cap n (s : State) (j : Z),
  Z.of_nat n = 256 - j -> 0 <= j < 256 ->
  InitInv inp cap s j -> WellFormed1 inp cap ->
  exists s', runUntil 0 (3 * n) s = s' /\ Pass1Entry inp cap s'.
Proof.
  intros inp cap n. induction n as [|n ih]; intros s j hn hj inv hwf.
  - exfalso. cbn in hn. lia.
  - destruct (init_iter inp cap s j inv hj hwf) as (s' & hrun & hpost).
    destruct (Z.ltb_spec (j + 1) 256) as [hlt|hge].
    + (* more iterations *)
      destruct (ih s' (j + 1) ltac:(lia) ltac:(lia) hpost hwf) as (s'' & hrun2 & hp2).
      exists s''. split; [| exact hp2].
      replace (3 * S n)%nat with (3 + 3 * n)%nat by lia.
      rewrite (runUntil_add 3 (3 * n) s), hrun, hrun2. reflexivity.
```

349	Lemma decodeS_nil : decodeS High [] = ([], Ok). Proof. now simp decodeS. Qed.
350	
351	Lemma readMem_eq : forall l m base,
352	  (forall j, (j < length l)%nat -> m (base + Z.of_nat j) = Z.of_nat (nth j l 0%nat)) ->
353	  readMem m base (length l) = l.
354	Proof.
355	  induction l as [|a l' IH]; intros m base H; simpl; [reflexivity|].
356	  f_equal.

358	    replace (base + Z.of_nat 0) with base in H by lia. simpl in H. rewrite H. apply Nat2Z.id.
359	  - apply IH. intros j Hj. specialize (H (S j) ltac:(simpl; lia)). simpl in H.
360	    rewrite <- H. f_equal. lia.
361	Qed.
362	
363	(** ** Loop invariant + the induction backbone (mirror of LoopInv/loop_correct).
364	
365	    Per the fuel-bound approach: each iteration runs <= 50 instructions per input
366	    char consumed, so the whole loop halts within [50 * |rest| + 4] steps -- a
367	    closed (non-existential) bound, so it composes with the fixed-fuel `runOn`. *)
368	
369	Record LoopInv (inp : list Z) (cap : Z) (s : State) (rest : list Z) (emitted : list nat) : Prop := {
370	  li_at_loop : s.(pc) = coreAddr + 8;
371	  li_code    : CodeLoaded s;
372	  li_a0      : rget s 10 = inputAddr;
373	  li_a1      : rget s 11 = Z.of_nat (length inp);
374	  li_a2      : rget s 12 = outAddr;
375	  li_a3      : rget s 13 = cap;
376	  li_ra      : rget s 1 = 0;
377	  li_in_mem  : forall j, 0 <= j < Z.of_nat (length inp) ->
378	                 s.(mem) (inputAddr + j) = nth (Z.to_nat j) inp 0;
379	  li_in_lt   : inputAddr + Z.of_nat (length inp) < 2 ^ 64;
380	  li_bytes   : forall b, In b inp -> 0 <= b < 256;
381	  li_in_fits : inputAddr + Z.of_nat (length inp) <= outAddr;
382	  li_out_lt  : outAddr + cap < 2 ^ 64;
383	  li_idx     : rget s 5 = Z.of_nat (length inp) - Z.of_nat (length rest);
384	  li_suffix  : skipn (length inp - length rest) inp = rest;
385	  li_outidx  : rget s 6 = Z.of_nat (length emitted);
386	  li_emit_le : (length emitted <= Z.to_nat cap)%nat;
387	  li_out_mem : forall j, (j < length emitted)%nat ->
388	                 s.(mem) (outAddr + Z.of_nat j) = Z.of_nat (nth j emitted 0%nat);

Lemma loop_prefix : forall inp cap c rest' emitted s,
  LoopInv inp cap s (c :: rest') emitted ->
  (runUntil 0 4 s).(pc) = coreAddr + 24 /\
  rget (runUntil 0 4 s) 7 = c /\
  rget (runUntil 0 4 s) 5 = rget s 5 + 1 /\
  (runUntil 0 4 s).(mem) = s.(mem) /\
  CodeLoaded (runUntil 0 4 s) /\
  (forall i, i <> 0 -> i <> 5 -> i <> 7 -> i <> 28 ->
     rget (runUntil 0 4 s) i = rget s i).
Proof.
  intros inp cap c rest' emitted s HI.
  destruct HI as [Hpc Hcode Ha0 Ha1 Ha2 Ha3 Hra Hinmem Hinlt Hbytes Hinfits Houtlt
                  Hidx Hsuf Houtidx Hemitle Houtmem Hspec].

  set (jZ := Z.of_nat (length inp) - Z.of_nat (length (c :: rest'))) in *.

    by (simpl length; lia).

    (hcode : CodeLoaded1 s)
    (hpc : s.pc = BitVec.ofNat 64 (Image1.coreAddr + off))
    (h1 : s.rget rs1 = BitVec.ofNat 64 A) (h2 : s.rget rs2 = BitVec.ofNat 64 A)
    (hd : Rv64i.decode (wordAt1 off) = Rv64i.Instr.bgeu rs1 rs2 immB)
    (ho : off + 3 < Image1.coreBytes.length)
    (htgt : BitVec.ofNat 64 (Image1.coreAddr + off) + immB.signExtend 64 = target) :
    step s = s.setPc target := by

        simp [BitVec.ult],
      hpc]

  isComment (Z.to_nat c) = true ->
  LoopInv inp cap s (c :: rest') emitted ->
  exists k, (exists rest'' emitted', (length rest'' < length (c :: rest'))%nat /\

### 🛠️ **Tool result**  ·  21:06:45; tool 99ms

```
Inductive Status1 := Ok1 | Split1 | Trailing1 | Unknown1 | Dup1 | Undef1 | TrailTok1.

(* Numeric status codes, matching the Error enum in hex1.c / core1.s. *)
Definition statusCode1 (s:Status1) : nat :=
  match s with
  | Ok1 => 0 | Split1 => 3 | Trailing1 => 4 | Unknown1 => 5
  | Dup1 => 6 | Undef1 => 7 | TrailTok1 => 8
  end.

(* The label map: label byte |-> output position. *)
```
